Of these three methods, one is that you make three fire cauterizations, or four, lining according to the length of the poison, according to the shape of the liver cauterization we have mentioned above; and do not press your hand on all the cauterization, so that the patient shudders on his back; and another method of cauterization is that you heat the cauterization which has two ends, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and apply the cauterization to the place where the cut of the patient comes towards the left, and let the elevation on which you apply the cauterization be according to the shape, according to the length of the spine, and the cauterization is according to the width of the spine.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After that, the two roots are heated until the burn is felt on the other side, and then the fire is quickly removed, and in doing so there will be three; and if you see it, cauterize to the whole root with three roots.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After he has gotten the wound by long time, and that is a must that the other before said cure get it.
de ydropisie	from hydrops
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	The cautery does not work for hydrops, except that which is called "ascultation.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat according to the ways we have said in the divisions, and your treatment does not benefit, then it is appropriate that you make three cauterizations around the body, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the back of the spine, and one on the navel; and let the cauterization be well placed to the skin of the cure.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leave the fire cautery to go away long time, and do not let the treatment of the disease after the cautery; and healing would hurry, and will be together the two intentions with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the fire cautery for the abdomen is the claw that we have before us to use; and this for the back is olive-shaped, according to what it is now described.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the pieces
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the pieces are swollen on the one who is hydrophylic, and they are plain of a yellow color, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the index and the middle finger; and lift your hand with the cautery without turning it back.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much too deeply, lest he should burn the yellow color, and the cautery is made according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe à la pointe dou cutellaire ; et soit li cauteres du long, l'un desoz le genoil devant et l'autre defuers, enmi la jambe ; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse ; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.
de la menoison	After doing the fire cautery on both legs up to the knuckle of the big toe, and making one cautery longer than the other, closer to the knee joint, leave the cauterizations in place for a long time without treating, because they will dry up  ; after that, treat the other leg in the same way.
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When a solution comes from cold and moisture, as long as the digestive and vitalizing power that is in the stomach and intestines remains afleboie [i.e., affluente, meaning 'abundant'], it cannot be cured by any kind of treatment; and you will see the patient suffer greatly and have great vitality, so make a large fire cautery on the stomach according to what has been said above about the fire cautery of the stomach, circulating it around; and four cauterizations around the navel very gently, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the sick suffering, then do fire cautery on his hand, and I cautery on each finger, and two small cauteries on the stomach to take away the great one, for the cure is helpful when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	for the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorrhoids are in the fundament, or one or more, and are old and have large cold and moist corrupting humors, and are cured as we have said in the divisions, and it does not benefit if fire cautery is done: three on the spine of the back, that which is all further down is cut little by little in a trialing manner, and one cautery is cut there II times; and if you think that his stomach is cold, and the meat does not cook, and inflammation appears on the face, then the face is given I great cautery on the stomach, as it is said before, and another on the liver, and another on the mouse at all the cauterized clavicles; and leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, leave the wound alone until it is well.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the carnage that is called "the flesh
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you treat the carnage, if it is hot, heat the cautery that seems like a razor, and then put it all on fire on the treated carnage; and leave it until the cautery comes to the birth of the vein, so that it does not hurt; do this once or twice, and if there is much carnage, cauterize each one as we have said; after treatment with beneficial ointments until they are well; and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the flesh, it will be more effective.
de plaie mal curee	of a wound that has not been properly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot tolerate cuts or openings, which we will describe in their place, if there comes a disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no opening for the vent, and it is raised up and there is putrifaction and moisture, then you must provide an entire subtle tent, and remember to know exactly how much the tent is perfect.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cautery which seems like a razor, and pouring it into the fistula according to the quantity that the tent has entered, and restarting the cauterization until the corruption and putrefaction of the skin are burned, once or twice, according to the quantity of the necessary application; and be careful of the nerves that are involved, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the back of the abdomen and the intestine, then be careful of these veins, and do not make a cut except in the meat, and think that it is not permanent; after treating the area until it is healthy, and if the matter has become stuck, and the bones have been exposed for a long time, then know that the vein is completely healthy; and if the matter has not become stuck, but the bone is corrupted at its base, then know that the vein is three-quarters healthy, and the bone is corrupted at its root; and in this way, as one of these that we will say in his place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When the pain of the kidneys and the great windiness comes, and does not take hold of a woman, then it is right that you make a fire cautery on both sides of the kidneys with the clava cautery which we have before said; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauterizes in line, and greater help will be done.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is soft and weak because of cold and moisture, so that the patient retenes urine, then you make a fire cautery in the back part on the bladder, where the hairs grow at the base, and one on each side, and let each be as long as an inch; and you make another fire cautery behind, where it is needed; and let the clava cauterys be made according to the form mentioned above.
de la marris	of the marrows
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the marrow is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are decayed and late in appearing; and when they do appear, there is great pain: therefore three cauterizations should be made around the loins, as we have said above for the cautery of the bladder, and two cauterizations on the back; and let the cauterization be clived, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip socket, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and the joints are found to be swollen, then you should cauterize the patient on the hip socket at the circle-like spot, and mark in front of the joint around the socket as it comes back together, so that the socket is within the circle; and if so, let the cautery be like those with which we have cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you do not have the fire caustice ready, then make three caustices of the olive oil, and make them complete like all the others; and heal as long as he is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the hip joint, and it is due to cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated as mentioned in the previous division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old: then you must purge the patient of the large humors with fetid pills, or other bad-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After that, make the caustice; and the manner of the caustice is as follows: namely, together with burning medicines, and fire caustice.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire caustice is according to many ways, of which one is: you should make three triangular caustices according to this shape, and make them deep and wide, and there between each caustice let the thickness of a thumb, and let the olive oil caustice; never do you make a caustice in the middle on top of the hip joint, for there are four according to this shape:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see, if the cautery is made with the ring that we have said above in the dislocation of the hip; but do it in such a way that the rings hold all the hip, and all the flesh of the cure is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain is located in the hip and does not reach until the thigh or only until the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it comes only to the thigh and leg, two cauterizations are made there where the patient feels the pain, and one cauterization above the ankle three times, five times at the most; and either the cauterization is done with a knife, and either the thickness of the flesh is burned; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two toes or almost to the ankle, cauterize there four times or five with the "poins" cautery.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if you do this profession, do it more; and if he says that the pain is in the groin towards the thigh, make a cauterization with the cautery knife or circular, and give him good care for all your cauterizations so that you don't let them go out so much with the cautery that you burn the nerves and the big arteries, and do not cause great harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have seen many who made a cauterization on the foot's sole, and left it so much that the leg was all swelled, and the toes too, and they were pierced and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal remedy from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two places together, make a cauterization in one and the other, according to this way.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the sage said in the cauterization of the heel, from which this is the way, make it one large as an nail of a finger, or slightly less, and put it between the intertrigemial spaces, and be the intertrigemia on both sides, and are also like nails, and there is one piece of iron well made; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And be heated until it is all red and hot, and then put it on the chest box of the sick leg, and turn it over the back side; and let him cauterize once, and he will cauterize and leave three days; and then make an ointment of butter, and leave the opened wound for a long time; after the cure of dressing until it is well.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Al-Buqaqum says that we use little of this cautery because of the risk of infection, and few who use it; but this is a good cautery, which can bear it, and let it be where it sticks.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The medical cauterization with hot instruments so that you make an instrument to pass through the edge of the door, and is of brass or iron with a long wall, and there are two of us, and there is a quantity of thickness of a finger on each side according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After you have treated the hip joint of the sick person lying on his side near the spine, and you have moved your hand very high up over the hip joint; after that you should enter between the two circles of hot awd which is heated with fire one pot, and leave it for an hour from now, and allow the patient to feel heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is the same as fire; and when the mortification has passed, you take off your hand with the instrument and raise the hip with soft awd, and leave it like that for three days, and put it on tar until what is black from the scald has grown out; and let it be three days to heal; and whoever is behind should help after the treatment of onions as long as he is well.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread only to the thigh or only to the leg, you make the instrument turn towards what you have done in the hip joint; and this is the way of hot awd, and I have written it and treated it with rectifying medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and live chalk, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together, and put them in a nine-pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Take alkali and live chalk, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together, and put them in a nine-pot. There should be a small opening at either end so that the powder can fall through; then place another pot, well sealed, on top of the alkali and chalk and add water gently to it, so that there are two layers of powder above the water; and leave it like this until the water is completely evaporated and the pot is empty, then take all the water out, and pour it over the chalk and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And then if it is very strong and very dry in the work of medicine and cautery of other members; for it does this work like fire, and with other medicines which well cauterize the skin together with resin, honey, almond, and soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galiens tells us of a cure wherein an honorable man was cured of the pain in the hip and sciatic vein, and he mowed his grass, and said that no other cure was made, and that he was healed on one soul when this cure was done, and he was bathed as it is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And he said in this way that you grind the green and dry barley, and mix it with a little fat, and put it on the hip and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is, and leave it; and let it lie for III hours, and by the quantity that the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then he puts it into the bath as long as his body is a little awake, and he puts him into bed, and the pain will go away all and will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery of such medicines, unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with a goat's hair, it should be done in this way; and the cautery must be made in such a manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take another and burn it with oil, and put it on the pit which is between the thumb and the other finger called the foist.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Afterwards take a dry goat' hair, and hold it to fire until it turns to ashes, and lay it on the wool, and leave it there until it is blackened; and then do it again, and never cease doing it as long as you think that it comes to the ankle, and the pain ceases; and this way of cauterizing is called "cauterizing with a goat' hair".
de la dolor dou dos	of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, or by chewing or from impact or from too much evacuation, or by the appearance of spread cold matter, none of these appearances is worth cauterizing, except that which comes from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	He must after that which the sick person is voiding of foul pills or others, be done to him on his back, where the pain holds, three lines marked with inch, and in each line five cauterizations or more according to virtue and quantity which the sick can suffer; and let the cauterization be made according to the cautery called 'pin'; and if you see, make three cauterizations or four at the cautery clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often comes about in small children, and the signs of the beginning are that he has a narrow back when he stands up, and he is afraid; and you will find in the last spine of the back and in us the appearance that comes over the others.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and when you have seen it, if you cure him with the cauldron of a cauldron according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the fire cautery is applied to each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you can see, then cauterize inside the spine with the burning cautery two or three lines, and let the burns be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After curing the area until it is healthy according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply the burn to a ganglion that is in the same place as a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the joints' pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the joints' pain is caused by moisture that spreads to each member of the body, and when the pain comes in pieces, which is called "gout" properly, and when it is caused by cold and cannot be cured with medicines, then it is cured with burns in this way: Make the burn of the cautery around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-colored according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary for you to touch on the face of the foot, then make fire cautery with all the fire cautery that is claimed "not".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come again to the genitals and other joints, and this happens many times, then make fire cautery on each testicle III cauterizes or IV of each part, with all the olive cautery; and if you need more, then do more, but do not hold your hand away from it except for as long as the skin of the cure is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend again to the genitals and the back, then administer the fire cautery that we have spoken of in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, then make a line with the fire II lines; and if there is still pain in the two, then make fire cautery on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come again to the arms or shoulders, then cauterize each part, and govern well the patient and apply medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you do good government and purge phlegm, then you will be healthy with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the treatment of disease
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the rupture comes in the ankles, and the balls descend like fresh grass, then it is necessary that when you look at him, he should not be able to move for a while; and he uses things that leave his belly cold, so that the end descends from his belly; after he sits down on his back between your hands, and orders him to wet his hair as long as his balls are repaired, and brings them back to your feet, and signs from above the rupture on the bone of the leg, and all is like a half-circle above the chest; then heat the cautery in such a way:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and drops water.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then return the balls to their place; and the assistant wet his hand so that it does not turn back; and well treat the legs of the sick person, and put a bag and a servant on the legs, and another one on his feet which wet his hands; then put the fire brand on all his hand, and hold it tight and hold it as long as you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, so you will start again a second time until you come to the bone; and be careful that the ball does not slip when you make the mark; that you do not burn it; and that by this sick person does not die, or another bad.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you come to the bone with the fire brand, your efforts are in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the fire brand of children be subtle according to their measure, and of great people also great according to their measure; after III days cure the place of the brand of butter until the heat is taken away; after the cure other oils until he is well, and let the sick person lie for 40 days on his back until the wound is well fixed; and it is necessary that his bandages be relaxed for a long time, so that the ball does not slide when he gets up to go to the chamber.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when he wants to get up, a well-made bandage is brought to him and applied for forty more days; and he should have good rest, so that he works little and guards against too much drinking and eating, and too much noise; and when he has done this teaching, then is he completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say here after the cure of the cutter in its paste.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture from the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they no longer grow, then do I cauterize the third of the cure according to its quantity, and let it be burned; after the cure according to what we have said; and no one of the elders has said that it should be cauterized at III angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the top of the incision and make a line across its width, and another on the other side, and with your hand push all the way down the nail.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterization is lighter and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any member, or from a blow or from a wound, and this pain persists for a long time, and the medicine cure does not help, then it is convenient that he be cauterized at the fire which is called "poins", and let the cauterization be according to the length of the member and its smallness and its feebleness and its virtue and its location from twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cauterization is well, that's good; but if not, restart another cauterization on that same member, for it is necessary that you make the cauterizations until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	of salivation
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The meself are aided by cauterization in a great way, and at most the disease that comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if there is any confusion everywhere; and it loses manifestly, so that you must cauterize this from the cauterization we said at the top of the head, and I cauterize in some neck, and II cauterize on the spine of the neck, and VI cauterize on the spine of the back, and I great one on the crown and another deliciously, and II on the two shoulders; and II on the blades, and II on the tendons of the foot, and I on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the creases of the hands; and guard against any burn that is on the back of the leg, so that you do not burn it; and never make a cauterization on the bone of the hand, and another one on the stomach bone, and another one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the more I make a caustic, the more aid I give and profit, and know that the patient does not feel the pain of the caustic as much as the healthy do because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the caustic be great and small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you will find in iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	Afterwards, cure him with flour of times with honey and other cures until he is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the swelling comes to any member and is cured with medicines, oils, and poultices, and it is not healthy, then make the cauterization on the member according to its size; and let the cauterization be a little inside the curative; and then cure it with ointments until it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And no time is there when cauterization should be made with the hand and foot and back, at the end of the nerve that moves the member, and so if it is osteal the swelling; but nevertheless do not meddle in it unless you know the members and the issues of the moving vessels.
de albaras	of scars
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and the medicine's power is useless, then cauterize with a fire cautery a little perfectly, according to the quantity of the spice of cure, until the blister is opened, and its color changes; then treat with flour of vesces and lentils with oil and plantain leaves, and blood of colon and almond, each in part; and mix them all together, and bind them with a cloth, and apply to the place until they are healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The cure for leprosy by cauterization:
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the leprosy appears at the beginning, and you see it stop, if the cautery with the fire seems a circle, all around the edge of the leprosy.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And always the wise men say that one should also cauterize in the middle of the leprosy; and this to me seems not good, for I fear it will become ulcers and rotten, and I have never seen this done at all; and more right is to cauterize around, with the fire called "circle," as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it delays dying or because of the excess blood the person has, or because he is very old and has little blood, or because of age; then you will see him hurry to die: then cauterize him with small fire cauteries by piercing him; then leave him like that.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hurry to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see him pierced all over with fire, so hot is the fire of this form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauterizes have pierced his pulse, and are such cauterizes that the patient feels cold in some way so that the course of corruption is controlled.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment as long as he is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	The fire cure by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of sickness is called "corrosion," and it is nothing other than a putrefaction of the limbs, for it eats away at the limbs just as fire dries up the wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in its early stages, treat it with fire simultaneously on all sides; then heat the fire cloves small and large according to what is appropriate for the place where the disease is; after fire treating from all sides until all corruption disappears, leaving nothing of it except that everything corrupted becomes bone.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days and put fire-treated clove broaches on top until the burns from the fire have healed and all corruption has disappeared.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment with garlic-based remedies that cause a burn.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that a boy does not come out healthy, it is good; and if he does not, let the cauterization begin again on him who has been delayed in his place corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this mentation is never once cured of medicine agony in place of fire cautery; but nevertheless, fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already said the cure of the medicine agony in the division: take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of onions that come to the stone
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	In many cases, it happens that because of the weather, a disease called "close" according to our intention appears, and is a large, foul thing that blisters the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization for this disease has two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to be understood cauterization by fire, and cauterization by hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Here is the translation of the text: 
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with poultice until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if the skin turns red and sometimes blisters, and there are many times that they come off and get stuck to something, then you should bring a hot water poultice; and in this way: take a hair from a horse or a iron, or a feather from a crow, and put it on the nail and the ointment, that is to say porpynx verrucae; and put the hair on it so that it turns red all around, then put some hot water on it, and hold your hand tight, and press your hand while turning it so that the edge of the hair comes to the root of the nail, and can find the hot water's path deeply up to the root; and let the patient feel a little burning from the hot water for an hour; then leave it like this, and it will come out all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Make another one like this until you have removed all those who are in the body, then heal the wounds that cause pain.
li cure dou trembler	He heals the trembling.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When some shiver from cold, or from a quarter fever or other, so that you make four or five cauterizations on the spine of the back, one cauterization between each spine; and one cauterization at the feet, and one cauterization on the stomach with olive oil; this will stop the shivering, and hasten the health from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled blisters.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No one appears on the body that has purulent pustules, which come from corrupted bulk.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If the first time that they appear one makes a cauterization on each head of the pustule: a thin cauterization with a twig of mistletoe, which is held in the fire, or a root of aristo long, or with a ring-shaped cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.
quant li artere est copee	And at no time are the cauterizations performed at the beginning when it appears, according to this method, and they cannot grow hair in advance, but the excess that comes is broken, and they are cured; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	For many times there is great pain of blood from the artery that is cut to the wound that comes to the surface, or to the incision of an abscess, or to the cauterization of the limb, and similar things; and it is a painful thing to stop it.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And in any case when it is done to anyone, if you are quick to put your little finger on the wound of a vein, and strain it as much as the blood stops flowing from it, and no more drops; then take fire with olive oil, large and small, as much as it is all red; then take I, or great or small according to the wound and place it in that place where you hold your little finger, and keep the cauterizer on it until the blood stops flowing.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if he pricks when you lie on your back, and the cauterization is finished, take quickly another of the cauterizations that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing one after the other as long as the blood is stopped; and beware that you do not burn the nerve which is delicate, and that another evil does not come upon the sick person; and know that when the artery stops [bleeding], it cannot be well stopped even if the artery is large, except by one of the four ways we have said: or by cauterization, or by extraction when it has not yet been treated, or by firmly tying a thread, or by medicines put on it which have the power to stop blood; and let it be bound and strained well.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer the stopping of the blood tightly with cloth or with burning things placed on it, or similar things, if he does not benefit from it, let him not do so.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	Et si ce arrive à aucun et il n'ait mie miré ne médecine présent, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nous avons dit, et bien étendre tant qu'il soit resté sur chés le plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou mouille d'avoine froide souvent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenéchis; et face des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cautères et de médecine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	And if this happens to anyone and he has not seen a physician or medicine, then he must put his second finger on the wound in the vein as we have said, and firmly stretch it over the wound and over the vein; and do not move it, but often moisten it with cold water until the blood is frozen and thickened and firm; and make incisions before those who need cauterization and medicine.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	Here begins the second book of cures for cuts and wounds; in which we will treat of fire cauterization, burning medicine, scrapings, causes, instruments, and shapes of cauterizations; and I have put this chapître from the root to the tip, and I will go into this chapître by that middle way for those who have a lighter wound to treat.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so, as I begin this, it is necessary, dear child, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauterizations, and for that reason greater caution is needed.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I forbid you to be foolish.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of doing things come about.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If they come from those who, with their disease, die easily because of the foolishness that they practice because of their disease, and because of its great severity, then one must be afraid of them.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And from these ones who give you your meaning, and say: "Wait, I am getting ready"; and the disease is a mockery.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is not appropriate that you consent to those who come to you who have this manner, but put more great trust in your honor than in your covetise, and do not open foolishly but carefully of him whom you are certain, and of whom you could have taken and lost; and use prophecy and indication in the treatment of your sick so that health is converted; and he who will help you to obtain good name, glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords give you good understanding and righteousness, and if you will seek the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter in speaking by chapters, according to the one who is before or the chapter of the cautery, which I have devised from the beginning up to the point, so that you can find more easily that of which you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	 dou chief plein d’aigue
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	I know that this disease often comes to infants when the mouth is drawn tight, and there is no reply for this reason:
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease come to anyone but children, and all those I have seen it affect die quickly; and by what I see, I should be more cautious in treating these cases.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw a child whose shoulder was swollen with water, and the head of the bone was pushing out through the skin every day until it could no longer be sustained; and the moisture was so great that he believed he would die, and this moisture had gathered between the joint and the bone, and the joint was very small, so that you would have to make a large cut in the head with a knife; and let it hang out as far as possible:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is greater, and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in a cross shape according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If the moisture has broken the bone, and you see the joints of the skull overflow on each side, and the liquid jumps out strongly when you press it with your hand, and it does not close again: then you should make three incisions in the skull according to this form:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture forcefully.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After, remove the bandages and powders, and put wine and oil on it, and leave it like that for five days; then remove it, and treat the wound with ointments and oils, and let the scalp be stripped evenly, and feed the patient dry meat because of the moisture as long as the limb is healed and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way to cut is that you look where the large part of the abscess is and the gathering of the sharp part; because it is not in front, nor behind, nor on the right, nor on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	So cut at the large part of the abscess and the gathering of the sharp part, and make an incision according to your ability; and be careful not to cover the artery; and let there be a flow of blood, so that the patient dies because of the blood loss and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	in conclusion
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	In conclusion: When there is a disease that is called "cataract" or "pit", and the disease is old, and the medical cure does not benefit, then the last cure is that of cauterization with what one will cover the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	It is necessary therefore, since you have covered the eyes, that the patient should raise his head; after which he rubs the place of a hard cloth until the arteries appear, and then removes the patient's collar from all the cloth; then see where the vein bites, and the lines of both are after the ears, and few are returned; then sign the lines of the chin, and then cover one and the other with a sharp spatumile from two sides, until the saw comes to the bone, and that may be through the large part of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, bottle the spatumile above the artery and cover it from above, cutting as well as two sides as a tree.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is covered, let it run upward constantly without ceasing.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open to the touch, then measure the quantity of the space of three fingers, and then sign the chin and cut up to the bone; and that which it is necessary to put fire on, so it is six-quarters, and perhaps a little more or less, according to what the patient can bear, and the expansion of the artery; then look at the wound: if it remains on the bone no syphac, if the cut apices do not i come, then extract the wound and bind, and the cure of ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of grinding
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the old grind comes, and catarrh is acquired, because of the moisture of tears and fever in the temples and ancient sore forsened and similar things, and it is medicated by the methods of medicine and all that does not benefit him, let us extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have told.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the way to extract them is that the patient does not let his hair grow in his temples, and listens to the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens very well with its pounding, and is not too tightly closed except in some men who are too cold; and if it is tightly closed, then the patient takes off some sheets, then he rubs the place with no rough cloth, and raises the place with hot water until the artery appears clearly; then take the spatulum where this is the form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then burn the skin lightly until you come to the artery, then draw it up as much as possible with pincers, and remove all the flesh that is attached to each part; and if the artery is small, turn it to the tip of the hook, then cut off that part according to the quantity of the two shoulders.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut off, then neither does the blood flow into all parts.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And draw blood from the six to three; and if the artery is large, then tie it with two strong threads of silk, so that blood does not come out before the wound heals, and comes out in turn; then, if you see, then cauterize with cautery cutellaire as far as the bone as soon as the shoulders are cut; and this is the operation of the doctor, if the patient does not have a fever and has a warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the fire cautery is an aid to stop moisture; for this is more of an aid than moisture itself.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	For the extraction of arteries, it is necessary to fill their place with wet cotton and put a well-made bandage on top; and when you remove them, use dry medicines that make charred bandages, and bandages, until they are healed; and if there is no stop to the artery as long as you work, quickly apply a cauterizing paste, or employ the juice of vitriol and strain it into your hand so that the stop is made; and if you do not have this present, put your finger in water as cold as possible for a long time, and remove it so that the stop is made as it should be; and the one that is bloody and heavier during the extraction of the artery is to be cauterized from both sides with a sharp instrument, but let the sharp instrument be well sharpened so that it lasts longer in heat.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too soft, then it keeps less of its heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it must have between the two tools a space of one inch, and then when you have sighed across the two lines, and you put on very hot iron as far as it comes to the bone, and cut the vein in two places; and be distant between the two shoulders because it is not souded by this cautery from top to bottom; and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears of the eyes descend from the veins that are on the forehead of the head of force, and this does not benefit from medicine that is made there, and you see the face of the sick person turn black, and feel a feverish movement as if it were shivers; and since they are soft and moist so that the hairs of the eyelids fall, and the eyelids are burned by the heat of the tears, and are scorched by the fire of the tear
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	Et let them call the ancient "cure for contusions", and that is that you make to rere to the patient who has this disease the hairs that he has or forehead, then he does III slits or forehead equally according to the length of the forehead; and be one of the slits as II doi all emmi the forehead in swallowing swallow until not ifef, and the others II at II costels by above the papers, and keep away from the incision of the arteries that are II costels by above the papers; and remove your hand from the continuation of the II mandibules, and be each wound the quantity of III does through joins; and have arranged a piece of sponge and many drapes her to essuer the blood, then bottle the sputum gained of II parts of where this is the form:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.
